line=189 tag=B:
line=190 tag=M:  6
line=191 tag=M:    A lexical accusative is ruled out by the fact that the promoted object does get nominative in the passive.
line=192 tag=M:  7
line=193 tag=M:    Accusative assignment is prima facie evidence for v/Agr2 in the unaccusative. We will see constructions
line=194 tag=M:  below where the passive must have a light verb; which seems independently needed to select the agent. I
line=195 tag=M:  accordingly follow Harley (1995), Legate (1998) in having light verbs in all intransitive constructions.
line=196 tag=M:  8
line=197 tag=M:    Pylkkänen (1998) argues that a passive light verb can assign Case.
line=198 tag=M:  9
line=199 tag=M:    It is also a reflexive pronoun and an "inherent" lexicalized morpheme.
